# Stage 2 re-tag ‚Äî proposed tag changes (diff report)

This report compares the tags each lesson has **today** with the tags the re-tagging run **proposes**. Nothing has been changed in the database ‚Äî this is a preview for review.

**How to read it:** each section covers one tag field. "Real changes" add or remove values; capitalization-only fixes (e.g. "winter" ‚Üí "Winter") are counted separately because they tidy formatting without changing what a lesson is about.

Grade levels are not compared in this report: the corpus export does not carry the lessons' current grade values, so the run's proposed grades are reviewed separately at the apply step.

## Coverage

- Lessons in the corpus export: 753
- Lessons excluded from the run (deletion-slated / not lessons, so never re-tagged): 12
- Lessons with a usable proposed tagging (compared below): 753
- Lessons without usable results: 0 (listed at the end)
- Run results that matched no corpus lesson: 0

## Activity Type

Out of the 753 lessons compared, 491 keep exactly the values they have today and 262 would genuinely change. The most common addition is "craft" (146 lessons); the most common removal is "garden" (105).

| | lessons |
|---|---|
| Same values as today | 491 |
| Real changes | 262 |
| Capitalization-only fixes | 0 |
| Empty before and after | 0 |

Most-added values:

- "craft" ‚Äî added to 146 lessons
- "academic" ‚Äî added to 22 lessons
- "cooking" ‚Äî added to 16 lessons
- "garden" ‚Äî added to 8 lessons

Most-removed values:

- "garden" ‚Äî removed from 105 lessons
- "cooking" ‚Äî removed from 33 lessons
- "academic" ‚Äî removed from 15 lessons

## Cultural Responsiveness Features

Out of the 753 lessons compared, 401 keep exactly the values they have today and 352 would genuinely change. The most common addition is "Promotes student-centered instruction" (101 lessons); the most common removal is "Incorporates different individual and cultural learning styles" (102).

| | lessons |
|---|---|
| Same values as today | 401 |
| Real changes | 352 |
| Capitalization-only fixes | 0 |
| Empty before and after | 1 |

- "Promotes student-centered instruction" ‚Äî added to 101 lessons
- "Encourages learning within the context of culture" ‚Äî added to 66 lessons
- "Reshapes curriculum" ‚Äî added to 44 lessons
- "Communicates high expectations" ‚Äî added to 34 lessons
- "Positions teacher as facilitator" ‚Äî added to 33 lessons
- "Incorporates different individual and cultural learning styles" ‚Äî added to 30 lessons

## Cooking Methods

Out of the 753 lessons compared, 457 keep exactly the values they have today and 296 would genuinely change. The most common addition is "basic-prep" (255 lessons); the most common removal is "stovetop" (34).

| | lessons |

## Observances & Holidays

Out of the 753 lessons compared, 611 keep exactly the values they have today and 140 would genuinely change. Another 2 only get capitalization fixes ‚Äî formatting cleanup, not a change in meaning. The most common addition is "Beginning of year" (61 lessons); the most common removal is "Black History Month" (14).
